Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204 Initiative to strengthen college and career readiness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204(1)(a): "College and career counseling" means:

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204(1)(a)(v): providing financial aid information; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204(1)(a)(vi): increasing understanding about college admission processes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204(1)(b): "LEA" or "local education agency" means a school district or charter school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204(2): There is created the Strengthening College and Career Readiness Program, a grant program for LEAs, to improve students' college and career readiness through enhancing the skill level of school counselors to provide college and career counseling.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-204(3)(a)(ii): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act is aligned with the Utah Comprehensive Counseling and Guidance Program as defined in rules established by the state board in accordance with

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205 Paraeducator to Teacher Scholarship Program -- Grants for math teacher training programs.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(1): 53E-6-102
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(1)(a): 53E-6-102 The terms defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(1)(b): As used in this section, "paraeducator" means a school employee who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(1)(b)(i): delivers instruction under the direct supervision of a teacher; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(1)(b)(ii): works in an area where there is a shortage of qualified teachers, such as special education, Title I, ESL, reading remediation, math, or science.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(2): The Paraeducator to Teacher Scholarship Program is created to award scholarships to paraeducators for education and training to become licensed teachers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(3): The state board shall use money appropriated for the Paraeducator to Teacher Scholarship Program to award scholarships of up to $5,000 to paraeducators employed by school districts and charter schools who are pursuing an associate's degree or bachelor's degree program to become a licensed teacher.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(4): A paraeducator is eligible to receive a scholarship if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(4)(a): the paraeducator is employed by a school district or charter school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(4)(b): is admitted to, or has made an application to, an associate's degree program or bachelor's degree program that will prepare the paraeducator for teacher licensure; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(4)(c): the principal at the school where the paraeducator is employed has nominated the paraeducator for a scholarship.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(a): The state board shall establish a committee to select scholarship recipients from nominations submitted by school principals.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(b): The committee shall include representatives of the state board, the Utah Board of Higher Education, and the general public, excluding school district and charter school employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(c): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(c)(i): 63A-3-106 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(c)(ii): 63A-3-107 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(c)(iii): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 rules made by the Division of Finance pursuant to Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(d): The committee shall select scholarship recipients based on the following criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(d)(i): test scores, grades, or other evidence demonstrating the applicant's ability to successfully complete a teacher education program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(5)(d)(ii): the applicant's record of success as a paraeducator.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(6): The maximum scholarship amount is $5,000.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7): Scholarship money may only be used to pay for tuition costs:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7)(a): of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7)(a)(i): an associate's degree program that fulfills credit requirements for the first two years of a bachelor's degree program leading to teacher licensure; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7)(a)(ii): the first two years of a bachelor's degree program leading to teacher licensure; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7)(b): at a higher education institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7)(b)(i): located in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(7)(b)(ii): accredited by the Northwest Commission on Colleges and Universities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(8): A scholarship recipient must be continuously employed as a paraeducator by a school district or charter school while pursuing a degree using scholarship money.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(9): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The state board shall make rules in accordance with this section and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(9)(a): scholarship application procedures;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(9)(b): the number of, and qualifications for, committee members who select scholarship recipients; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(9)(c): procedures for distributing scholarship money.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10): If the state obtains matching funds of equal sums from private contributors, the state board may award grants to institutions of higher education or nonprofit educational organizations for programs that provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a): mentoring and training leading to a secondary education license with a certificate in mathematics for an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a)(i): is not a teacher in a public or private school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a)(ii): does not have a teaching license;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a)(iii): has a bachelor's degree or higher; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a)(iv): demonstrates a high level of mathematics competency by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a)(iv)(A): successfully completing substantial course work in mathematics; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(a)(iv)(B): passing a mathematics content exam; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(10)(b): a stipend, professional development, and leadership opportunities to an experienced mathematics teacher who demonstrates high content knowledge and exemplary teaching and leadership skills to assist the teacher in becoming a teacher leader.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(11): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(11)(a): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The state board shall make rules in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-205(11)(b): In awarding grants, the state board shall consider the amount or percent of matching funds provided by the grant recipient.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209 Grants for school-based mental health supports.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(1): 35A-9-102 As used in this section:

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(2): (3) Subject to legislative appropriations and Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(3)(a): first priority to an LEA that proposes to target funds to one or more elementary schools with a high percentage of students exhibiting risk factors for childhood trauma; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(3)(b): second priority to an LEA that proposes to target funds to one or more elementary schools with a high percentage of students experiencing intergenerational poverty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(4): (4)(a)(i) To qualify for a grant, an LEA shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(4)(a): (4)(a)(i) submit an application to the state board that includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(4)(a)(i): measurable goals on improving student safety, student engagement, school culture, and academic achievement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(4)(a)(ii): (4)(a)(i) how the LEA intends to meet goals submitted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(4)(b): provide local funds to match grant funds received under this section in an amount equal to one-half of the amount of the grant funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(5): An LEA may not replace federal, state, or local funds previously allocated to employ qualified personnel with funds distributed under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(6): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (7) In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(6)(a): procedures for applying for and awarding grants under this section, including:

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(6)(a)(iii): a schedule for submission of matching grant funds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(6)(b): (7) annual reporting requirements for grantees in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(7): (4)(a)(i) An LEA that receives a grant under this section shall submit an annual report to the state board, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(7)(a): (4)(a)(i) progress toward achieving the goals submitted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(7)(b): if the LEA decides to discontinue the qualifying personnel position, the LEA's reason for discontinuing the position.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-209(8): Beginning on or before July 1, 2019, the state board shall provide training that instructs educators on the impact of trauma on student learning, including information advising educators against practicing medicine, giving a diagnosis, or providing treatment.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218 Grow Your Own Educator Pipeline Program.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(a): "Paraprofessional" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(a)(i): works with students in an LEA as a paraprofessional or in a similar teaching assistant position; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(a)(ii): is not licensed to teach.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(b): "Program" means the Grow Your Own Educator Pipeline Program that this section creates.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(c): "School counselor" means an educator who is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(c)(i): licensed as a school counselor in accordance with state board rule; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(c)(ii): assigned to provide direct and indirect services to students in accordance with a school counseling program model that the state board provides.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(d): "School counselor assistant" means a student who is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(d)(i): enrolled in an accredited bachelor's degree program in a related field; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(d)(ii): completing the student's practicum experience in a school counseling department under the supervision of a licensed school counselor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(e): "School counselor intern" means a student who is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(e)(i): enrolled in an accredited school counselor master's degree program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(e)(ii): completing the student's hours of a supervised counseling internship by applying appropriate school counseling techniques under the supervision of a licensed school counselor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(f): "School psychologist" means an individual:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(f)(i): whom the state board licenses to practice as a school psychologist; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(f)(ii): who is assigned to provide direct and indirect services to students within the relevant school or LEA seeking program grant funding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(g): "School social worker" means an individual:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(g)(i): whom the state board licenses as a school social worker; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(g)(ii): who is assigned to provide direct and indirect services to students within the relevant school or LEA seeking program grant funding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(1)(h): "Teacher" means an educator who has an assignment to teach in a classroom.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(2): The Grow Your Own Educator Pipeline Program is a competitive grant program created to provide funding to LEAs to award scholarships to paraprofessionals, teachers, school counselor assistants, and school counselor interns within the LEA for education and training to become licensed teachers, licensed school counselors, licensed school psychologists, or licensed school social workers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(3)(a): The state board shall use money appropriated for the program to provide funding to LEAs that are awarded grants under the program to award scholarships to eligible candidates.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(3)(b): The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(3)(b)(i): determine the amount of an award an LEA receives under the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(3)(b)(ii): prioritize the amount of an award an LEA receives based upon an LEA's identified need.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(3)(c): The principal within the participating LEA shall nominate a candidate for the scholarship awarded under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4): (5); (4)(b)(i)(A) An LEA that participates in the program may select a candidate for a scholarship award if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(a): the candidate is a resident of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b): (5); (4)(b)(i)(A)
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(i): (5); (4)(b)(i)(A) for a paraprofessional:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(i)(A): a school district or a charter school has employed the candidate as a paraprofessional for at least one year before entering the program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(i)(B): (5); (4)(b)(i)(A) subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(ii): for a teacher, the candidate:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(ii)(A): was a paraprofessional who was awarded a scholarship;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(ii)(B): was offered employment as a teacher before the teacher completed the training to become a professionally licensed teacher; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(ii)(C): is working as a teacher for the same LEA where the teacher previously worked as a paraprofessional and was awarded the scholarship;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(iii): for a school counselor assistant, the candidate:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(iii)(A): is enrolled in a bachelor's degree program in a related field; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(iii)(B): demonstrates a commitment to continue the school counselor assistant's education after graduation in school counseling;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(iv): for a school counselor intern, the candidate is enrolled in a school counselor master's degree program accredited by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(iv)(A): the Council for Accreditation of Counseling and Related Educational Programs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(iv)(B): another regionally recognized accrediting body that meets the state board's standards for school counselor education programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(v): for a school psychologist student, including a student, practicum student, or intern, the candidate is enrolled in a school psychology education specialist or doctorate program that the National Association of School Psychologists accredits; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(4)(b)(vi): for a candidate studying to become a school social worker, including a student or practicum intern, the candidate is enrolled in a masters level social work program that the Council of Social Work Education accredits.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(5): (4)(b)(i)(B) The percentage of an LEA's paraprofessional scholarship recipients who are eligible for a scholarship using equivalent experience under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(6): A scholarship award under the program may only be used for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(6)(a): tuition, books, fees, and certification tests for required coursework and licensure;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(6)(b): stipends for mentors or school counselor assistants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(6)(c): if the LEA pays 0.15 of a full-time equivalent and all employee benefits, payment of a 0.35 full-time equivalent for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(6)(c)(i): a paraprofessional, up to one semester of student teaching; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(6)(c)(ii): a school counselor assistant or school counselor intern, up to two semesters of practicum or internship hours.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(7): An LEA shall ensure that a paraprofessional scholarship recipient is continuously employed as a paraprofessional by the paraprofessional's LEA while pursuing a degree using scholarship money under the program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; 53G-4-410 The state board shall make rules in accordance with this section and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8)(a): grant and scholarship application procedures;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8)(b): procedures for distributing scholarship money;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8)(c): assignment and eligibility of qualified mentors;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8)(d): stipends for mentors or school counselor assistants;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8)(e): 53G-4-410 administrative costs for regional education service agencies, as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-218(8)(f): eligibility requirements for potential candidates for scholarships regarding the completion of the Free Application for Federal Student Aid and the acceptance of other grants, tuition or fee waivers, and scholarships offered to the candidate.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220 School Safety and Support Grant Program -- Rulemaking.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1): The state board may award a grant to an LEA in response to an LEA request for proposal to provide a school with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(a): school resource officer services;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(b): school safety specialists and school safety specialist training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(c): safety and security training by law enforcement agencies for school employees;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(d): interoperable communication hardware, software, equipment maintenance, and training for first responder communication systems;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(e): enhanced physical security at a school upon completion of the school's threat assessment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(f): first-aid kits for classrooms; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(1)(g): bleeding control kits.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(2): An LEA may not apply for a grant under this section to fund services already in place, but an LEA may submit a request for proposal to fund an expansion of or enhancement to existing services.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-220(3): The state board shall prioritize grant funding for LEAs with low student counts that have designated a school safety specialist in each school.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221 Management of energy and water use pilot program.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(1)(a): "Energy" means natural gas or electricity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(1)(b): "Great Salt Lake watershed" means the drainage area for the Great Salt Lake, the Bear River watershed, the Jordan River watershed, the Utah Lake watershed, the Weber River watershed, and the West Desert watershed.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(1)(c): "Rural school district or charter school" means a school district or charter school that is located within a county of the third, fourth, fifth, or sixth class.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2): (5)
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2)(a): (5) On or after May 3, 2023, but before July 1, 2028, the state board may award a grant to a school district or charter school upon recommendation by the review panel created in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2)(b): When issuing a grant under this section, the state board shall prioritize outdoor water conservation projects.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2)(c): When issuing a grant under this section during the period beginning on May 3, 2023, and ending October 31, 2023, the state board shall prioritize, in the order the state board considers appropriate, a grant:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2)(c)(i): to a rural school district or charter school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2)(c)(ii): to a school district or charter school that is located within the Great Salt Lake watershed; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(2)(c)(iii): for an outdoor water conservation project.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3): (3)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a): Grant money may be used to pay for any of the following, provided the use is directly related to reducing the use of energy or water by the school district or charter school:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(i): computer equipment and peripherals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(ii): software;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(iii): upgrades of existing computer equipment or software;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(iv): physical equipment used to deliver energy or water;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(v): upgrades of existing physical equipment used to deliver energy or water;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(vi): personnel to provide technical support or coordination and management;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(vii): staff or student management training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(viii): recalibration of equipment for increased efficiency; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(a)(ix): another means of optimizing and measuring energy or water efficiency.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(3)(b): (3)(a) Equipment or software purchased in compliance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4)(a): establishing procedures for applying for and awarding a grant;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4)(b): establishing eligibility criteria;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4)(c): creating grant distribution thresholds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4)(d): specifying how grant money is allocated among school districts and charter schools;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4)(e): requiring reporting of grant money expenditures and evidence showing that the grant money has been used to implement reduced use of energy or water; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(4)(f): establishing technology standards.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(5): The state board shall establish a review panel to consider grant applications under this section, which shall include in addition to a representative for the state board, representation from the Office of Energy Development, the Department of Environmental Quality, the Division of Water Resources, and private energy providers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-221(6): By no later than the 2027 November interim meeting of the following, the state board shall report on the effectiveness of grants issued under this section to the following:

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(1): "Eligible elementary school" or "eligible junior high school" means a district school or charter school that has at least 50% of the school's students with a family income at or below 185% of the federal poverty level.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2): "Eligible partnership" means a partnership that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a): includes at least:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(i): a local education agency that has designated an eligible school feeder pattern;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(ii): a local nonprofit organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(iii): a private business;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(iv): a municipality or county in which the eligible school feeder pattern is located;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(v): an institution of higher education within the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(vi): a state or local government agency that provides services to students attending schools within the eligible school feeder pattern;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(vii): a local philanthropic organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(a)(viii): a local health care organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(2)(b): has designated a local education agency or local nonprofit organization to act as lead applicant for a grant described in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(3): (3)(a); (3)(a); (3)(a); (3)(b) "Eligible school feeder pattern" means the succession of schools that a student enrolls in as the student progresses from kindergarten through grade 12 that includes, as designated by a local education agency:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(3)(a): a high school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(3)(b): (3)(a); (3)(a) an eligible junior high school that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-401(3)(b)(i): (3)(a) is a district school within the geographic boundary of the high school described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402 Partnerships for Student Success Grant Program established.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(1): There is created the Partnerships for Student Success Grant Program to improve educational outcomes for low income students through the formation of cross sector partnerships that use data to align and improve efforts focused on student success.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2): 53E-3-1003; 53F-5-403 Subject to legislative appropriations, the state board shall award grants to eligible partnerships that enter into a memorandum of understanding between the members of the eligible partnership to plan or implement a partnership that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a): 53E-3-1003 establishes shared goals, outcomes, and measurement practices based on unique community needs and interests that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(i): 53E-3-1003 for students attending an elementary school within an eligible school feeder pattern, focus on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(i)(A): kindergarten readiness;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(i)(B): 53E-3-1003 reading proficiency, consistent with the science of reading, as defined by the science of reading panel described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(i)(C): grade 3 mathematics; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(ii): for students attending a secondary school within an eligible school feeder pattern, focus on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(ii)(A): grade 8 mathematics and reading proficiency;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(ii)(B): high school graduation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(ii)(C): postsecondary education attainment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(ii)(D): physical and mental health; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(a)(ii)(E): development of career skills and readiness;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(b): coordinates and aligns services to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(b)(i): students attending schools within an eligible school feeder pattern; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(b)(ii): the families and communities of the students within an eligible school feeder pattern;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(c): implements a system for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(c)(i): sharing data to monitor and evaluate shared goals and outcomes, in accordance with state and federal law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(c)(ii): accountability for shared goals and outcomes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(2)(d): 53F-5-403 commits to providing matching funds as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(3): In making grant award determinations, the state board shall prioritize funding for an eligible partnership that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(3)(a): focus on early literacy and mathematics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(3)(b): includes a low performing school as determined by the state board; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(3)(c): addresses parent and community engagement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(4): 53F-5-401 In awarding grants under this part, the state board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(4)(a): 53F-5-401 shall distribute funds to the lead applicant designated by the eligible partnership as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-402(4)(b): may not award more than $500,000 per fiscal year to an eligible partnership.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-406 Rules.
--------------------------------------
In accordance with

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(1): "Blended learning" means a formal education program in which a student learns:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(1)(a): at least in part, through online learning with some element of student control over time, place, path, and pace;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(1)(b): at least in part, in a supervised brick-and-mortar location away from home; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(1)(c): in a program in which the modalities along each student's learning path within a course or subject are connected to provide an integrated learning experience.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(2): "Extended learning" means learning opportunities outside of a traditional school structure, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(2)(a): online learning available anywhere, anytime;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(2)(b): career-based experiences, including internships and job shadowing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(2)(c): community-based projects; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(2)(d): off-site postsecondary learning.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(3): "Grant program" means the Personalized, Competency-Based Learning Grants Program created in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(4): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5): "Personalized, competency-based learning" means a system of learning in which the following principles influence the daily actions of the educational community:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(a): students are empowered daily to make important decisions about the students' learning experiences, how the students will create and apply knowledge, and how students will demonstrate the students' learning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(b): assessment is a meaningful, positive, and empowering learning experience for students that yields timely, relevant, and actionable evidence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(c): students receive timely, differentiated support based on the students' individual learning needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(d): students progress based on evidence of mastery rather than by hours of attendance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(e): students learn actively using different pathways and varied pacing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(f): strategies to ensure equity for all students are embedded in the culture, structure, and pedagogy of schools and education systems; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(5)(g): rigorous, common expectations for learning, including knowledge, skills, and dispositions, are explicit, transparent, measurable, and transferable.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(6): 53F-5-502 "Review committee" means the committee established under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-501(7): "STEM" means science, technology, engineering, and mathematics.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502 Personalized Competency-Based Learning Grants Program -- State board duties -- Review committee -- Technical assistance training.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(1): There is created the Personalized Competency-Based Learning Grants Program consisting of the grants created in this part to improve educational outcomes in public schools  through personalized, competency-based learning.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(2): The grant program shall incentivize an LEA to establish personalized, competency-based learning within the LEA through the use of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(2)(a): personalized learning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(2)(b): blended learning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(2)(c): extended learning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(2)(d): educator professional learning in personalized, competency-based learning; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(2)(e): any other method that emphasizes personalized, competency-based learning.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (4) The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(a): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(a)(i): for the administration of the grant program and awarding of grants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(a)(ii): to define outcome-based measures appropriate to the type of grant for an LEA that is awarded a grant under this part to use to measure the performance of the LEA's plan or program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(b): establish a grant application process;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(c): (4) in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(c)(i): metrics to analyze the quality of a grant application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(c)(ii): approval of a grant application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(3)(d): with input from the review committee, adopt metrics to analyze the quality of a grant application.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(4)(a): The review committee shall consist of STEM and blended learning experts, current and former school administrators, current and former teachers, and at least one former school district superintendent, in addition to other staff designated by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(4)(b): The review committee shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(4)(b)(i): review a grant application submitted by an LEA;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(4)(b)(ii): make recommendations to the LEA to modify the application, if necessary; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(4)(b)(iii): make recommendations to the state board regarding the final disposition of an application.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(a): The state board shall provide technical assistance training to assist an LEA with a grant application under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(b): An LEA may not apply for a grant under this part unless:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(b)(i): a representative of the LEA attends the technical assistance training before the LEA submits a grant application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(b)(ii): the representative is a superintendent, principal, or a person in a leadership position within the LEA.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(c): The technical assistance training shall include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(c)(i): instructions on completing a grant application, including grant application requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(c)(ii): information on the scoring metrics used to review a grant application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(5)(c)(iii): information on personalized, competency-based learning.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-502(6): The state board may use up to 5% of an appropriation provided to fund this part for administration of the grant program.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506 Waiver from state board rule -- State board recommended statutory changes.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act An LEA may apply to the state board in a grant application submitted under this part for a waiver of a state board rule made in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(2): The state board may grant the waiver, unless:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(2)(a): the waiver would cause the LEA to be in violation of state or federal law; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(2)(b): the waiver would threaten the health, safety, or welfare of students in the LEA.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(3): If the state board denies the waiver, the state board shall provide in writing the reason for the denial to the waiver applicant.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(4): (4)(a); 53E-1-203
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(4)(a): The state board shall request from each LEA that receives a grant under this part for each year the LEA receives funds:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(4)(a)(i): information on a state statute that hinders an LEA from fully implementing the LEA's program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-506(4)(a)(ii): suggested changes to the statute.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507 Cooperation of institutions of higher education -- Transferring students not to be penalized.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507(1): An institution of higher education:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507(1)(a): shall, for purposes of admission, scholarships, and other financial aid consideration, recognize and accept on equal footing as a traditional high school diploma a high school diploma awarded to a student who successfully completes an educational program that uses, in whole or in part, personalized, competency-based learning; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507(1)(b): cooperate with an LEA:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507(1)(b)(i): as applicable, to facilitate the advancement of a student who attends a personalized, competency-based learning program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507(1)(b)(ii): as requested, in the development of an LEA plan or program under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-507(2): If a student attending an LEA that establishes personalized, competency-based learning within the LEA transfers to another school within the LEA or to another LEA entirely that does not have a personalized, competency-based learning program, the student may not be penalized by being required to repeat course work that the student has successfully completed, changing the student's grade, or receive any other penalty related to the student's previous attendance in the personalized, competency-based learning program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-601 Definitions.

As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-601(1): "American Indian and Alaskan Native concentrated school" means a school where at least 29% of the school's students are American Indian or Alaskan Native.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-601(2): 36-22-1 "Native American Legislative Liaison Committee" means the committee created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-601(4): "Teacher" means an individual employed by a school district or charter school who is required to hold an educator license issued by the state board and who has an assignment to teach in a classroom.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-602 Program created.
------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-602(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-602(1)(a): In addition to the state plan adopted under
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-602(1)(b): The program shall consist of a grant program to school districts and charter schools to be used to fund stipends, recruitment, retention, and professional development of teachers who teach in American Indian and Alaskan Native concentrated schools.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-602(1)(c): In determining grant recipients for at least two-thirds of the money appropriated to the program, the state board shall give priority to American Indian and Alaskan Native concentrated schools located in a county of the fourth, fifth, or sixth class with significant populations of American Indians and Alaskan Natives.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-5-602(2): Up to 3% of the money appropriated to the grant program under this part may be used by the state board for costs in implementing the program.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-403 Qualifying providers.
-----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-403(1): Before the beginning of the school year immediately following a school year in which a qualifying provider receives scholarship funds equal to or more than $500,000, the qualifying provider shall file with the program manager a surety bond payable to the program manager in an amount equal to the aggregate amount of scholarship funds expected to be received during the school year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-403(2): If a program manager determines that a qualifying provider has violated a provision of this part, the program manager may interrupt disbursement of or withhold scholarship funds from the qualifying provider.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406 Qualifying provider regulatory autonomy -- Home school autonomy -- Student records -- Scholarship student status.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(1): Nothing in this part:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(1)(a): except as expressly described in this part, grants additional authority to any state agency or LEA to regulate or control:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(1)(a)(i): a private school, qualifying provider, or home school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(1)(a)(ii): students receiving education from a private school, qualifying provider, or home school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(1)(b): applies to or otherwise affects the freedom of choice of a home school student, including the curriculum, resources, developmental planning, or any other aspect of the home school student's education; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(1)(c): expands the regulatory authority of the state, a state office holder, or an LEA to impose any additional regulation of a qualifying provider beyond any regulation necessary to administer this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(2): A qualifying provider:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(2)(a): has a right to maximum freedom from unlawful governmental control in providing for the educational needs of a scholarship student who attends or engages with the qualifying provider; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(2)(b): is not an agent of the state by virtue of the provider's acceptance of payment from a scholarship account in accordance with this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(3): 53F-6-403; 53F-6-408; 53F-6-409 Except as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(4): Title 53E, Chapter 9, Student Privacy and Data Protection An LEA or a school in an LEA in which a scholarship student was previously enrolled shall provide to the scholarship student's parent a copy of all school records relating to the student that the LEA possesses within 30 days after the day on which the LEA or school receives the parent's request for the student's records, subject to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(4)(a): Title 53E, Chapter 9, Student Privacy and Data Protection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(4)(b): Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1232g.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(5): By virtue of a scholarship student's involvement in the program and unless otherwise expressly provided in statute, a scholarship student is not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(5)(a): enrolled in the public education system; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-406(5)(b): otherwise subject to statute, administrative rules, or other state regulations as if the student was enrolled in the public education system.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408 Eligible schools.
-------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1): 53G-11-402; Title 53E, Chapter 6, Education Professional Licensure To be eligible to receive scholarship funds on behalf of a scholarship student as an eligible school, a private school with 150 or more enrolled students shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(a)(i): contract with an independent licensed certified public accountant to conduct an agreed upon procedures engagement as the state board adopts, or obtain an audit and report that:

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(a)(i)(C): audits financial statements from within the 12 months immediately preceding the audit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(a)(ii): submit the audit report or report of the agreed upon procedure to the program manager when the private school applies to receive scholarship funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(b): comply with the antidiscrimination provisions of 42 U.S.C. Sec. 2000d;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(c): provide a written disclosure to the parent of each prospective scholarship student, before the student is enrolled, of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-408(1)(c)(i): the education services that the school will provide to the scholarship student, including the cost of the provided services;

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412 Reports.
----------------------------------------
Beginning in 2025 and in accordance with SectionUtah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1): 53F-6-405 the program manager shall submit a report on the program to the Education Interim Committee no later than September 1 of each year that includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(a): the total amount of tuition and fees qualifying providers charged for the current year and previous two years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(b): the total amount of goods paid for with scholarship funds in the previous year and a general characterization of the types of goods;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(c): administrative costs of the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(d): 53F-6-405 the number of scholarship students from each county and the aggregate number of eligible students on the waitlist described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(e): the percentage of first-time scholarship students who were enrolled in a public school during the previous school year or who entered kindergarten or a higher grade for the first time in Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(f): the program manager's strategy and outreach efforts to reach eligible students whose family income is at or below 200% of the federal poverty level and related obstacles to enrollments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(g): in the report that the program manager submits in 2025, information on steps the program manager has taken and processes the program manager has adopted to implement the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(1)(h): any other information regarding the program and the program's implementation that the committee requests; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-412(2): the state board shall submit a report on the cost-effectiveness of the program to the Education Interim Committee no later than September 1 of each year.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413 Legal proceedings.
--------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(1): In any legal proceeding against the state in which a qualifying provider challenges the application of this part to the qualifying provider, the state shall bear the burden of establishing that the law:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(1)(a): is necessary; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(1)(b): does not impose an undue burden on the qualifying provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(2): The following bear no liability based on the award or use of scholarship funds under this part:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(2)(a): the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(2)(b): the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(2)(c): the program manager; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(2)(d): an LEA.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-413(3): If any provision of this part is the subject of a state or federal constitutional challenge in a state court, scholarship students and scholarship students' parents may intervene as a matter of right to defend the program's constitutionality, subject to any court order that all defending parents and scholarship students intervene jointly.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-414 Severability.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-414(1): If any provision of this part or the application of any provision of this part to any person or circumstance is held invalid by a final decision of a court of competent jurisdiction, the remaining provisions of this part remain effective without the invalidated provision or application.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-414(2): The provisions of this part are severable.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-6-415 Procurement flexibility.
--------------------------------------------------------
For the year 2023, if the state board determines that it is not feasible to successfully meet a procurement and contracting deadline in this part, the state board may extend the deadline by no more than 90 days.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53F - Chapter 7 - State Funding -- Education Administration

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-7-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "State Funding -- Education Administration."

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-7-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-7-201 Appropriations from Automobile Driver Education Tax Account.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
There is appropriated to the state board from the Automobile Driver Education Tax Account, annually, all money in the account, in excess of the expense of administering the collection of the tax, for use and distribution in the administration and maintenance of driver education classes and programs with respect to classes offered in the school district and the establishment of experimental programs, including the purchasing of equipment, by the state board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-8-202 Levy of tax -- Collection and deposit.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-8-202(1): 53F-8-201 After the valuation of property has been extended on the assessment rolls, the county legislative body shall levy a tax on the taxable property in the respective school districts at the rate submitted by each local school board under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-8-203 Payment out of tax money by county treasurer.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-8-203(2): The treasurer shall make payment as quickly as possible after collection or realization.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53F - Chapter 9 - Funds and Accounts
****************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Funds and Accounts."

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-103 Nonlapsing funds.
-------------------------------------------------
All appropriations to the state board are nonlapsing, including appropriations to the Minimum School Program and all agencies, line items, and programs under the jurisdiction of the state board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201 Uniform School Fund -- Contents -- Trust Distribution Account.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1): 53D-1-401 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(a): "Annual distribution calculation" means, for a given fiscal year, the average of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(a)(i): 4% of the average market value of the State School Fund for that fiscal year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(a)(ii): the distribution amount for the prior fiscal year, multiplied by the sum of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(a)(ii)(A): one;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(a)(ii)(B): the percent change in student enrollment from the school year two years prior to the prior school year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(a)(ii)(C): the actual total percent change of the consumer price index during the last 12 months as measured in June of the prior fiscal year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(b): "Average market value of the State School Fund" means the results of a calculation completed by the SITFO director each fiscal year that averages the value of the State School Fund for the past 20 consecutive quarters ending in the prior fiscal year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(c): "Consumer price index" means the Consumer Price Index for All Urban Consumers: All Items Less Food & Energy, as published by the Bureau of Labor Statistics of the United States Department of Labor.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(e)(i): the annual distribution calculation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-9-201(1)(e)(ii): 4% of the average market value of the State School Fund.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102 Capital development project proposal process -- State board role.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The state board shall make rules, in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(1)(a): the panel's review, prioritization, and recommendation to the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(1)(b): the state board's consideration and approval, if applicable, of proposed capital development projects; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(1)(c): management of panel processes and administration.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(2): The state board may fund direct costs and administration of the panel, not to exceed $200,000.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(3): The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(3)(a): evaluate recommendations of the panel regarding proposed capital development projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(3)(b): approve proposed capital development projects, subject to the availability of capital development funding; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-102(3)(c): oversee the disbursement of capital development funding.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202 Panel duties.
----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1): 53F-10-301; 53F-10-302; 53F-2-304 The panel shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a): 53F-10-301; 53F-10-302; 53F-2-304 determine criteria for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a)(i): 53F-10-301; 53F-10-302; 53F-2-304 the allowed uses of capital project fund resources described in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a)(i)(A): eliminates risks to student life and safety through renewal or replacement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a)(i)(B): 53F-2-304 enhances efficiency of use, including combining necessarily existent small schools, described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a)(i)(C): addresses essential program growth and capacity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a)(i)(D): provides a cost effective solution that is appropriate for the facility's need; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(a)(i)(E): comports with the school district's provision of matching funds and sufficient revenues for ongoing operation and maintenance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(b): evaluate capital development project proposals to ensure viability, efficiency, and adherence to education and construction standards;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(c): prioritize capital development projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(d): recommend that the state board distribute capital project funding to school districts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(e): if necessary based on the circumstances of the capital development project, in partnership with the division, oversee the capital development project; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(1)(f): report to the state board regarding the panel's actions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(2): The panel may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(2)(a): determine that a technical assistance liaison is necessary for an eligible school district applying for capital project funding under this chapter to efficiently complete the project; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-202(2)(b): facilitate engagement with the division or a willing school district partner having the required technical expertise in similar capital development projects.


Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301 Capital development project grants.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1): (1)(b); (1)(a); (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a): (1)(b) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(i): for an eligible school district with a capital local levy rate of at least 0.00105, up to 50% of the total cost of the capital development project as a 1:1 matching grant;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(ii): for an eligible school district with a capital local levy rate of at least 0.0015, up to 66.67% of the total cost of the capital development project as a 2:1 matching grant;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(iii): for an eligible school district with a capital local levy rate of at least 0.0018, up to 75% of the total cost of the capital development project as a 3:1 matching grant;
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(iv): for an eligible school district with a capital local levy rate of at least 0.00225, up to 80% of the total cost of the capital development project as a 4:1 matching grant; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(v): up to 100% of the total cost of the capital development project as a non-matching grant for an eligible school district that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(v)(A): has incurred debt equal to 90% of the debt limit imposed by
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(a)(v)(B): unless the school district's capital local levy rate is at least 0.00225, increases the school district's capital local levy by 10% after March 24, 2022.
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(1)(b): (1)(a); (1)(a) Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(2): (1) The panel shall determine the terms of a grant described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-301(3): A school district that receives grant funding under this section shall demonstrate the ability to provide sufficient ongoing funding to support the operation and maintenance of the new or renovated facility resulting from the capital development project based on standards that the panel establishes.

Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-302(1)(b)(ii): that has incurred debt equal to 90% of the debt limit imposed by
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-302(2): (1) The panel shall determine the repayment terms of a loan described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-302(3): (1) Repayment of a loan described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53F-10-302(4): An LEA that receives loan funding under this section shall demonstrate the ability to provide sufficient ongoing funding to support the operation and maintenance of the new or renovated facility resulting from the capital development project based on standards that the panel establishes.
